   1: import AxeBuilder from "@axe-core/playwright";
   2: import { expect, test } from "@playwright/test";
   3: 
   4: /**
   5:  * Phase 2C.5 — WCAG 2.2-AA accessibility audit.
   6:  *
   7:  * For each user-facing route we run axe-core with the WCAG 2A + 2AA + 2.1AA
   8:  * + 2.2AA + best-practice rule sets and assert zero violations. Any new
   9:  * violation should fail CI rather than silently regress accessibility.
  10:  *
  11:  * Failure mode is intentionally LOUD — if axe surfaces a violation we
  12:  * print the rule id, impact, and the affected node selectors so the fix
  13:  * is one click away.
  14:  */
  15: 
  16: const WCAG_TAGS = [
  17:   "wcag2a",
  18:   "wcag2aa",
  19:   "wcag21a",
  20:   "wcag21aa",
  21:   "wcag22aa",
  22:   "best-practice",
  23: ];
  24: 
  25: async function expectNoA11yViolations(page: import("@playwright/test").Page) {
  26:   const results = await new AxeBuilder({ page }).withTags(WCAG_TAGS).analyze();
  27: 
  28:   if (results.violations.length > 0) {
  29:     const summary = results.violations
  30:       .map(
  31:         (v) =>
  32:           `\n  - [${v.impact}] ${v.id}: ${v.description}\n    nodes: ${v.nodes
  33:             .map(
  34:               (n) =>
  35:                 n.target.join(" ") +
  36:                 (n.failureSummary
  37:                   ? ` — ${n.failureSummary.replace(/\n/g, " ")}`
  38:                   : ""),
  39:             )
  40:             .join("\n           ")}`,
  41:       )
  42:       .join("");
  43:     throw new Error(
  44:       `axe-core found ${results.violations.length} WCAG-AA violation(s):${summary}`,
  45:     );
  46:   }
  47: }
  48:

  50:   test("/dashboard initial render is WCAG-AA clean", async ({ page }) => {
  51:     await page.goto("/dashboard", { waitUntil: "networkidle" });
  52:     await expectNoA11yViolations(page);
  53:   });

 161: test.describe("WCAG 2.5.8 target-size sweep (F-28 — broader than axe)", () => {
 162:   // axe's target-size rule has loose overlap-detection; cycle-8 P1.1 and
 163:   // P1.4 surfaced multiple <button>/<label>/<a role="button"> surfaces
 164:   // that pass axe but fail strict WCAG 2.2 SC 2.5.8 AA (24x24 minimum).
 165:   // This sweep walks every clickable element + asserts ≥24x24 directly.
 166: 
 167:   test("Dashboard — all clickable targets ≥24x24", async ({ page }) => {
 168:     await page.goto("/dashboard", { waitUntil: "networkidle" });
 169:     const small = await page.evaluate(() => {
 170:       const results: Array<{
 171:         tag: string;
 172:         text: string;
 173:         w: number;
 174:         h: number;
 175:       }> = [];
 176:       // Exclude <label htmlFor=...> — labels paired with a form control
 177:       // delegate the hit target to the control itself (WCAG 2.5.8 "inline"
 178:       // exemption). The "browse files" label has no htmlFor (it wraps the
 179:       // hidden file input directly) so it remains in scope.
 180:       const sel =
 181:         'button, label:not([for]), [role="button"], [role="radio"], a[href]';
 182:       document.querySelectorAll(sel).forEach((el) => {
 183:         if (!(el instanceof HTMLElement)) return;
 184:         const r = el.getBoundingClientRect();
 185:         if (r.width === 0 || r.height === 0) return; // hidden / pre-render
 186:         if (r.width < 24 || r.height < 24) {
 187:           results.push({
 188:             tag: el.tagName,
 189:             text: (el.textContent || "").trim().slice(0, 60),
 190:             w: Math.round(r.width),
 191:             h: Math.round(r.height),
 192:           });
 193:         }
 194:       });
 195:       return results;
 196:     });
 197:     if (small.length > 0) {
 198:       throw new Error(
 199:         `WCAG 2.5.8 failures (${small.length} target(s) < 24x24):\n` +
 200:           small
 201:             .map((s) => `  - ${s.tag} "${s.text}" → ${s.w}x${s.h}px`)
 202:             .join("\n"),
 203:       );
 204:     }
 205:   });

   6: "use client";

   8: import { ArrowRight, FileSearch, Plus } from "lucide-react";
   9: import Link from "next/link";
  10: import { useEffect, useState } from "react";
  11: 
  12: import {
  13:   EmptyState,
  14:   ErrorState,
  15:   LoadingState,
  16: } from "@/components/states/state_kit";
  17: import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button";
  18: import { listCompletedRuns, type RunStatusResponse } from "@/lib/api";
  19: 
  20: type LoadState =
  21:   | { kind: "loading" }
  22:   | { kind: "ok"; runs: RunStatusResponse[] }
  23:   | { kind: "error"; message: string };
  24: 
  25: function formatWhen(value: string | null | undefined): string | null {
  26:   if (!value) return null;
  27:   const d = new Date(value);
  28:   if (Number.isNaN(d.getTime())) return null;
  29:   return d.toLocaleDateString(undefined, {
  30:     month: "short",
  31:     day: "numeric",
  32:     year: "numeric",
  33:   });
  34: }
  35: 
  36: // Honest verdict label: lifecycle `status` cannot distinguish a success from an
  37: // abort (mark_aborted stores status=completed) — pipeline_status is the truth.
  38: function verdictOf(run: RunStatusResponse): { label: string; cls: string } {
  39:   const v = run.pipeline_status ?? run.status;
  40:   if (v === "success") {
  41:     return {
  42:       label: "Verified",
  43:       cls: "text-verified border-verified/30 bg-verified/10",
  44:     };
  45:   }
  46:   if (typeof v === "string" && v.startsWith("abort_")) {
  47:     return {
  48:       label: "Declined",
  49:       cls: "text-refusal-foreground border-refusal/30 bg-refusal/10",
  50:     };
  51:   }
  52:   if (typeof v === "string" && v.startsWith("error_")) {
  53:     return {
  54:       label: "Error",
  55:       cls: "text-destructive border-destructive/30 bg-destructive/10",
  56:     };
  57:   }
  58:   return {
  59:     label: v ?? "Unknown",
  60:     cls: "text-muted-foreground border-border bg-muted/30",
  61:   };
  62: }
  63: 
  64: export default function DashboardPage() {
  65:   const [state, setState] = useState<LoadState>({ kind: "loading" });
  66: 
  67:   useEffect(() => {
  68:     let cancelled = false;
  69:     (async () => {
  70:       try {
  71:         const runs = await listCompletedRuns(50);
  72:         if (!cancelled) setState({ kind: "ok", runs });
  73:       } catch (err) {
  74:         if (!cancelled) {
  75:           setState({
  76:             kind: "error",
  77:             message:
  78:               err instanceof Error
  79:                 ? err.message
  80:                 : "Could not load runs from the backend.",
  81:           });
  82:         }
  83:       }
  84:     })();
  85:     return () => {
  86:       cancelled = true;
  87:     };
  88:   }, []);
  89: 
  90:   return (
  91:     <section
  92:       data-testid="dashboard-page"
  93:       className="mx-auto flex w-full max-w-5xl flex-col gap-6 px-6 py-10"
  94:     >
  95:       <div className="flex flex-wrap items-end justify-between gap-4">
  96:         <div className="flex flex-col gap-1">
  97:           <h1 className="text-foreground text-2xl font-semibold tracking-tight sm:text-3xl">
  98:             Runs
  99:           </h1>
 100:           <p className="text-muted-foreground text-sm">
 101:             Recent verified research briefs. Open one to replay its proof, claim
 102:             by claim.
 103:           </p>
 104:         </div>
 105:         <Button
 106:           nativeButton={false}
 107:           className="h-10"
 108:           render={
 109:             <Link href="/intake" data-testid="dashboard-start-run">
 110:               <Plus aria-hidden className="mr-1.5 h-4 w-4" />
 111:               Start new research
 112:             </Link>
 113:           }
 114:         />
 115:       </div>
 116: 
 117:       {state.kind === "loading" ? (
 118:         <LoadingState label="Loading runs…" rows={5} />
 119:       ) : null}
 120: 
 121:       {state.kind === "error" ? (
 122:         <ErrorState title="Couldn't load runs" message={state.message} />
 123:       ) : null}
 124: 
 125:       {state.kind === "ok" && state.runs.length === 0 ? (
 126:         <EmptyState
 127:           icon={FileSearch}
 128:           title="No runs yet"
 129:           description="Once you run a research question, every verified brief shows up here for monitoring and replay."
 130:           action={
 131:             <Button
 132:               nativeButton={false}
 133:               variant="outline"
 134:               render={<Link href="/intake">Start your first research</Link>}
 135:             />
 136:           }
 137:         />
 138:       ) : null}
 139: 
 140:       {state.kind === "ok" && state.runs.length > 0 ? (
 141:         <ul
 142:           className="border-border divide-border divide-y rounded-xl border"
 143:           data-testid="runs-list"
 144:         >
 145:           {state.runs.map((run) => {
 146:             const verdict = verdictOf(run);
 147:             const when = formatWhen(run.finished_at ?? run.queued_at);
 148:             return (
 149:               <li key={run.run_id}>
 150:                 <Link
 151:                   href={`/runs/${run.run_id}`}
 152:                   data-testid={`run-row-${run.run_id}`}
 153:                   className="hover:bg-muted/40 focus-visible:ring-ring/70 flex items-center justify-between gap-4 px-4 py-3 transition-colors focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:outline-none"
 154:                 >
 155:                   <div className="flex min-w-0 flex-col gap-1">
 156:                     <span className="text-foreground line-clamp-1 text-sm font-medium">
 157:                       {run.question || run.run_id}
 158:                     </span>
 159:                     <span className="text-muted-foreground text-xs">
 160:                       <span className="text-primary font-medium tracking-wide uppercase">

 162:                       </span>

  77: export interface RunRequest {
  78:   template: TemplateId;
  79:   question: string;
  80:   document_ids?: string[];
  81: }
  82: 
  83: export interface RunStatusResponse {
  84:   run_id: string;
  85:   status: RunStatus;
  86:   // I-ui-bug-001 (#725): the pipeline-A verdict (success / abort_* / partial_*
  87:   // / error_*), distinct from the lifecycle `status`. mark_aborted() stores
  88:   // lifecycle_status='completed' for aborts, so lifecycle alone CANNOT tell a
  89:   // successful run from an aborted one — pipeline_status is required to render
  90:   // a completed run honestly (an aborted run must NOT show as success).
  91:   pipeline_status?: string | null;
  92:   // I-rdy-011 (#507): true once a cancel has been requested; lets the run
  93:   // page show a cancel as in-flight before an in-progress run transitions.
  94:   cancel_requested?: boolean;
  95:   template: string;
  96:   question: string;
  97:   queued_at: string;
  98:   started_at?: string | null;
  99:   finished_at?: string | null;
 100: }
 101: 
 102: export interface ApiError extends Error {
 103:   status: number;
 104:   body: unknown;
 105: }
 106: 
 107: async function asJsonOrThrow<T>(response: Response): Promise<T> {
 108:   const body = await response.json().catch(() => null);
 109:   if (!response.ok) {
 110:     const error = new Error(
 111:       `POLARIS backend returned ${response.status}`,
 112:     ) as ApiError;
 113:     error.status = response.status;
 114:     error.body = body;
 115:     throw error;
 116:   }
 117:   return body as T;
 118: }
 119: 
 120: /**
 121:  * Thrown by createRun when POST /runs is rejected by the 1-concurrent-session
 122:  * constraint (I-rdy-013): a research run is already queued or in progress.
 123:  */
 124: export class ConcurrentRunError extends Error {
 125:   readonly activeRunId: string;
 126:   readonly activeStatus: string;
 127:   constructor(message: string, activeRunId: string, activeStatus: string) {
 128:     super(message);
 129:     this.name = "ConcurrentRunError";
 130:     this.activeRunId = activeRunId;
 131:     this.activeStatus = activeStatus;
 132:   }
 133: }
 134: 
 135: export async function createRun(
 136:   payload: RunRequest,
 137: ): Promise<RunStatusResponse> {
 138:   const response = await authFetch(`${BACKEND_URL}/runs`, {
 139:     method: "POST",
 140:     headers: { "content-type": "application/json" },
 141:     body: JSON.stringify(payload),
 142:   });
 143:   if (response.status === 409) {
 144:     // Read the body exactly once, then unwrap FastAPI's { detail: {...} }
 145:     // envelope. The 1-concurrent-session reject carries a structured detail;
 146:     // any other 409 falls through to a generic ApiError.
 147:     const body = (await response.json().catch(() => null)) as {
 148:       detail?: unknown;
 149:     } | null;
 150:     const detail = (body?.detail ?? body) as {
 151:       code?: string;
 152:       message?: string;
 153:       active_run_id?: string;
 154:       active_status?: string;
 155:     } | null;
 156:     if (detail && detail.code === "concurrent_run_active") {
 157:       throw new ConcurrentRunError(
 158:         detail.message ?? "A research run is already in progress.",
 159:         detail.active_run_id ?? "",
 160:         detail.active_status ?? "in_progress",
 161:       );
 162:     }
 163:     const error = new Error("POLARIS backend returned 409") as ApiError;
 164:     error.status = 409;
 165:     error.body = body;
 166:     throw error;
 167:   }
 168:   return asJsonOrThrow<RunStatusResponse>(response);
 169: }
 170: 
 235:   only_right_frames: string[];
 236:   left_contradictions: number;
 237:   right_contradictions: number;
 238:   pipeline_status_match: boolean;
 239:   family_segregation_both_pass: boolean;
 240: }
 241: 
 242: export async function listCompletedRuns(
 243:   limit = 20,
 244: ): Promise<RunStatusResponse[]> {
 245:   const response = await authFetch(
 246:     `${BACKEND_URL}/runs?status=completed&limit=${limit}`,
 247:   );
 248:   return asJsonOrThrow<RunStatusResponse[]>(response);
 249: }
 250: 
 251: export async function compareRuns(
 252:   left: string,
 253:   right: string,
 254: ): Promise<ReportComparison> {
 255:   const response = await authFetch(
 256:     `${BACKEND_URL}/runs/${encodeURIComponent(left)}/compare/${encodeURIComponent(right)}`,
 257:   );
 258:   return asJsonOrThrow<ReportComparison>(response);
 259: }

+function formatWhen(value: string | null | undefined): string | null {
+  if (!value) return null;
+  const d = new Date(value);
+  if (Number.isNaN(d.getTime())) return null;
+  return d.toLocaleDateString(undefined, {
+    month: "short",
+    day: "numeric",
+    year: "numeric",
+  });

+// abort (mark_aborted stores status=completed) — pipeline_status is the truth.
+function verdictOf(run: RunStatusResponse): { label: string; cls: string } {
+  const v = run.pipeline_status ?? run.status;
+  if (v === "success") {
+    return {
+      label: "Verified",
+      cls: "text-verified border-verified/30 bg-verified/10",
+    };
+  }
+  if (typeof v === "string" && v.startsWith("abort_")) {
+    return {
+      label: "Declined",
+      cls: "text-refusal-foreground border-refusal/30 bg-refusal/10",
+    };
+  }
+  if (typeof v === "string" && v.startsWith("error_")) {
+    return {
+      label: "Error",
+      cls: "text-destructive border-destructive/30 bg-destructive/10",
+    };
+  }
+  return {
+    label: v ?? "Unknown",
+    cls: "text-muted-foreground border-border bg-muted/30",
+  };
